msg:Convenient transportation, adjacent to the highway. The hotel is the No.1 in the local area on the platform. The front desk service is enthusiastic. The room was upgraded. It is very spacious and bright. The indoor lighting layout is warm. Because it is a change of seasons, the air conditioner has no cooling mode and only fresh air. The windows are fully closed, so the room is a bit stuffy. There is a Chinese restaurant on the second floor where you can order food, but there is no small table for individual guests, only large tables. The price of the dishes is not low, and the quality of the ingredients and the cooking level are a bit lacking. For example, the beef cubes are not only glutenous but also woody, the vegetables are salty, and the dishes are slow to come out, which is inconsistent with the brand advertised. The price of the dishes is high, and the expectations of the guests are high. If there is no strength or carelessness, dissatisfaction is inevitable. The five-star reviews of the front desk and the guest rooms were pulled down by the catering. There are many varieties of buffet breakfast, and the quality is acceptable. There is no self-service laundry room, only laundry service.
